  <span m="4191040">our</span> <span m="4191130">project</span> <span m="4191529">is</span>
  <span m="4191850">to</span> <span m="4192010">design</span> <span m="4193130">a</span>
  <span m="4193240">system</span> <span m="4193729">that</span> <span m="4193890">allows</span>
  <span m="4194229">her</span> <span m="4194520">to</span> <span m="4194810">call</span>
  <span m="4195110">for</span> <span m="4195270">help.</span> <span m="4196430">Currently</span>
  <span m="4196930">the</span> <span m="4197050">system</span> <span m="4197610">in</span>
  <span m="4197760">place</span> <span m="4198100">in</span> <span m="4198170">The</span>
  <span m="4198250">Boston</span> <span m="4198570">Home</span> <span m="4199240">is</span>
  <span m="4199460">just</span> <span m="4199780">inaccessible</span> <span m="4200710">for</span>
  <span m="4201060">a</span> <span m="4201430">large</span> <span m="4202000">percentage</span>
  <span m="4202380">of</span> <span m="4202480">the</span> <span m="4202590">time.</span>
  <span m="4203530">Currently,</span> <span m="4203920">it''s</span> <span m="4204240">a</span>
  <span m="4204330">button</span> <span m="4204710">that''s</span> <span m="4204880">attached</span>
  <span m="4205290">to</span> <span m="4205330">the</span> <span m="4205430">wall,</span>
  <span m="4206000">and</span> <span m="4206460">when</span> <span m="4206620">you''re</span>
  <span m="4206720">pulling</span> <span m="4207240">the</span> <span m="4207350">drawer</span>

  <span m="4209310">found.</span> <span m="4210360">So</span> <span m="4210650">we</span>

  <span m="4212800">we</span> <span m="4212980">call</span> <span m="4213220">it</span>
